Header not set\")\n   362→\t} else if len(tenantids) > 1 {\n   363→\t\t// Loki supports multiple tenant IDs, but we should receive them from different contexts\n   364→\t\tlogger.Error(strconv.Itoa(len(tenantids)) + \" tenant IDs found. to map the SupportingQueryType to the actual header value. For\n\t// legacy reasons we defined each value, such as \"logsVolume\" maps to the\n\t// \"logvolhist\" header value to Loki. Header not set\")\n\t\treturn req\n\t}\n\n\ttenantids := md.Get(\"tenantid\")\n\tif len(tenantids) == 0 {\n\t\t// We assume we are not using multi-tenant mode, which is fine\n\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Tenant ID not present. Header not set\")\n\t} else if len(tenantids) > 1 {\n\t\t// Loki supports multiple tenant IDs, but we should receive them from different contexts\n\t\tlogger.Error(strconv.Itoa(len(tenantids)) + \" tenant IDs found. Header not set\")\n\t} else {\n\t\treq.Header.Add(\"X-Scope-OrgID\", tenantids[0])\n\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Tenant ID \" + tenantids[0] + \" added to Loki request\")\n\t}\n\treturn req\n}\n","numLines":371,"startLine":1,"totalLines":371}}}

46→func makeDataRequest(ctx context.Context, lokiDsUrl string, query lokiQuery) (*http.Request, error) {\n    47→\tqs := url.Values{}\n    48→\tqs.Set(\"query\", query.Expr)\n    49→\n    50→\tqs.Set(\"direction\", string(query.Direction))\n    51→\n    52→\t// MaxLines defaults to zero when not received,\n    53→\t// and Loki does not like limit=0, even when it is not needed\n the\n   150→\t// value of that field.\n   151→\t// but, the response might be just a simple string,\n   152→\t// this was used in older Loki versions.\n   153→\t// so our approach is this:\n   154→\t// - we try to convert the bytes to JSON\n   155→\t// - we take the value of the field \"message\"\n   156→\t// - if any of these steps fail, or if \"message\" is empty, we return the whole text\n   157→\n   158→\treturn makeLokiError(bytes)\n   159→}\n   160→\n   161→func (api *LokiAPI) DataQuery(ctx context.Context, query lokiQuery, responseOpts ResponseOpts) (*backend.DataResponse, Header not set\")\n   362→\t} else if len(tenantids) > 1 {\n   363→\t\t// Loki supports multiple tenant IDs, but we should receive them from different contexts\n   364→\t\tlogger.Error(strconv.Itoa(len(tenantids)) + \" tenant IDs found. Header not set\")\n   362→\t} else if len(tenantids) > 1 {\n   363→\t\t// Loki supports multiple tenant IDs, but we should receive them from different contexts\n   364→\t\tlogger.Error(strconv.Itoa(len(tenantids)) + \" tenant IDs found. := prometheus.AlreadyRegisteredError{}\n   108→\t\tif errors.As(err, &promError) {\n   109→\t\t\treturn promError.ExistingCollector\n   110→\t\t}\n   111→\t\tpanic(err)\n   112→\t}\n   113→\treturn c\n   114→}\n   115→\n   116→// Client pushes entries to Loki and can be stopped\n   117→type Client interface {\n   118→\tChan() chan<- Entry\n   119→\n   120→\tStop()\n   121→\tStopNow()\n   122→}\n   123→\n   124→// Client for pushing logs in snappy-compressed protos over HTTP.\n   125→type client struct {\n   126→\tmetrics *metrics\n   127→\tlogger  log.Logger\n   128→\tcfg     Config\n   129→\tclient  *http.Client\n   130→\tentries chan Entry\n   131→\n   132→\tonce sync.Once\n   133→\twg   sync.WaitGroup\n   134→\n   135→\t// ctx is used in any upstream calls from the `client`.\n   136→\tctx    context.Context\n   137→\tcancel context.CancelFunc\n   138→}\n   139→\n   140→// Tripperware can wrap a roundtripper.\n   141→type Tripperware func(http.RoundTripper) http.RoundTripper\n   142→\n   143→// New makes a new Client.\n   144→func New(reg prometheus.Registerer, cfg Config, logger log.Logger) (Client, error) {\n   145→\treturn newClient(reg, cfg, logger)\n   146→}\n   147→\n   148→func newClient(reg prometheus.Registerer, cfg Config, logger log.Logger) (*client, error) {\n   149→\tif cfg.URL.URL == nil {\n   150→\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"client needs target URL\")\n   151→\t}\n   152→\n   153→\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n   154→\n   155→\tc := &client{\n   156→\t\tlogger:  logger.New(\"host\", cfg.URL.Host),\n   157→\t\tcfg:     cfg,\n   158→\t\tentries: make(chan Entry),\n   159→\t\tmetrics: newMetrics(reg),\n   160→\n   161→\t\tctx:    ctx,\n   162→\t\tcancel: cancel,\n   163→\t}\n   164→\n   165→\terr := cfg.Client.Validate()\n   166→\tif err != nil {\n   167→\t\treturn nil, err\n   168→\t}\n   169→\n   170→\tc.client, err = config.NewClientFromConfig(cfg.Client, \"promtail\", config.WithHTTP2Disabled())\n   171→\tif err != nil {\n   172→\t\treturn nil, err\n   173→\t}\n   174→\n   175→\tc.client.Timeout = cfg.Timeout\n   176→\n   177→\t// Initialize counters to 0 so the metrics are exported before the first\n   178→\t// occurrence of incrementing to avoid missing metrics.\n   179→\tfor _, counter := range c.metrics.countersWithHost {\n   180→\t\tcounter.WithLabelValues(c.cfg.URL.Host).Add(0)\n   181→\t}\n   182→\n   183→\tc.wg.Add(1)\n   184→\tgo c.run()\n   185→\treturn c, nil\n   186→}\n   187→\n   188→// NewWithTripperware creates a new Loki client with a custom tripperware.\n   189→func NewWithTripperware(reg prometheus.Registerer, cfg Config, logger log.Logger, tp Tripperware) (Client, error) {\n   190→\tc, err := newClient(reg, cfg, logger)\n   191→\tif err != nil {\n   192→\t\treturn nil, err\n   193→\t}\n   194→\n   195→\tif tp != nil {\n   196→\t\tc.client.Transport = tp(c.client.Transport)\n   197→\t}\n   198→\n   199→\treturn c, nil\n   200→}\n   201→\n   202→func (c *client) run() {\n   203→\tbatches := map[string]*batch{}\n   204→\n   205→\t// Given the client handles multiple batches (1 per tenant) and each batch\n   206→\t// can be created at a different point in time, we look for batches whose\n   207→\t// max wait time has been reached every 10 times per BatchWait, so that the\n   208→\t// maximum delay we have sending batches is 10% of the max waiting time.\n   209→\t// We apply a cap of 10ms to the ticker, to avoid too frequent checks in\n   210→\t// case the BatchWait is very low.\n   211→\tminWaitCheckFrequency := 10 * time.Millisecond\n   212→\tmaxWaitCheckFrequency := c.cfg.BatchWait / 10\n   213→\tif maxWaitCheckFrequency < minWaitCheckFrequency {\n   214→\t\tmaxWaitCheckFrequency = minWaitCheckFrequency\n   215→\t}\n   216→\n   217→\tmaxWaitCheck := time.NewTicker(maxWaitCheckFrequency)\n   218→\n   219→\tdefer func() {\n   220→\t\tmaxWaitCheck.Stop()\n   221→\t\t// Send all pending batches\n   222→\t\tfor tenantID, batch := range batches {\n   223→\t\t\tc.sendBatch(tenantID, batch)\n   224→\t\t}\n   225→\n   226→\t\tc.wg.Done()\n   227→\t}()\n   228→\n   229→\tfor {\n   230→\t\tselect {\n   231→\t\tcase e, ok := <-c.entries:\n   232→\t\t\tif !ok {\n   233→\t\t\t\treturn\n   234→\t\t\t}\n   235→\t\t\ttenantID := c.getTenantID(e.Labels)\n   236→\t\t\tbatch, ok := batches[tenantID]\n   237→\n   238→\t\t\t// If the batch doesn't exist yet, we create a new one with the entry\n   239→\t\t\tif !ok {\n   240→\t\t\t\tbatches[tenantID] = newBatch(e)\n   241→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   242→\t\t\t}\n   243→\n   244→\t\t\t// If adding the entry to the batch will increase the size over the max\n   245→\t\t\t// size allowed, we do send the current batch and then create a new one\n   246→\t\t\tif batch.sizeBytesAfter(e) > c.cfg.BatchSize {\n   247→\t\t\t\tc.sendBatch(tenantID, batch)\n   248→\n   249→\t\t\t\tbatches[tenantID] = newBatch(e)\n   250→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   251→\t\t\t}\n   252→\n   253→\t\t\t// The max size of the batch isn't reached, so we can add the entry\n   254→\t\t\tbatch.add(e)\n   255→\n   256→\t\tcase <-maxWaitCheck.C:\n   257→\t\t\t// Send all batches whose max wait time has been reached\n   258→\t\t\tfor tenantID, batch := range batches {\n   259→\t\t\t\tif batch.age() < c.cfg.BatchWait {\n   260→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   261→\t\t\t\t}\n   262→\n   263→\t\t\t\tc.sendBatch(tenantID, batch)\n   264→\t\t\t\tdelete(batches, tenantID)\n   265→\t\t\t}\n   266→\t\t}\n   267→\t}\n   268→}\n   269→\n   270→func (c *client) getTenantID(labels model.LabelSet) string {\n   271→\t// Check if it has been overridden while processing the pipeline stages\n   272→\tif value, ok := labels[ReservedLabelTenantID]; ok {\n   273→\t\treturn string(value)\n   274→\t}\n   275→\n   276→\t// Check if has been specified in the config\n   277→\tif c.cfg.TenantID != \"\" {\n   278→\t\treturn c.cfg.TenantID\n   279→\t}\n   280→\n   281→\t// Defaults to an empty string, which means the X-Scope-OrgID header\n   282→\t// will not be sent\n   283→\treturn \"\"\n   284→}\n   285→\n   286→func (c *client) Chan() chan<- Entry {\n   287→\treturn c.entries\n   288→}\n   289→\n   290→func (c *client) sendBatch(tenantID string, batch *batch) {\n   291→\tbuf, entriesCount, err := batch.encode()\n   292→\tif err != nil {\n   293→\t\tc.logger.Error(\"error encoding batch\", \"error\", err)\n   294→\t\treturn\n   295→\t}\n   296→\tbufBytes := float64(len(buf))\n   297→\tc.metrics.encodedBytes.WithLabelValues(c.cfg.URL.Host).Add(bufBytes)\n   298→\n   299→\tbackoff := backoff.New(c.ctx, c.cfg.BackoffConfig)\n   300→\tvar status int\n   301→\tfor {\n   302→\t\tstart := time.Now()\n   303→\t\t// send uses `timeout` internally, so `context.Background` is good enough.\n   304→\t\tstatus, err = c.send(context.Background(), tenantID, buf)\n   305→\n   306→\t\tc.metrics.requestDuration.WithLabelValues(strconv.Itoa(status), c.cfg.URL.Host).Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n   307→\n   308→\t\t// Only retry 429s, 500s and connection-level errors.\n   309→\t\tif status > 0 && status != 429 && status/100 != 5 {\n   310→\t\t\tbreak\n   311→\t\t}\n   312→\n   313→\t\tc.logger.Warn(\"error sending batch, will retry\", \"status\", status, \"error\", err)\n   314→\t\tc.metrics.batchRetries.WithLabelValues(c.cfg.URL.Host).Inc()\n   315→\t\tbackoff.Wait()\n   316→\n   317→\t\t// Make sure it sends at least once before checking for retry.\n   318→\t\tif !backoff.Ongoing() {\n   319→\t\t\tbreak\n   320→\t\t}\n   321→\t}\n   322→\n   323→\tif err != nil {\n   324→\t\tc.logger.Error(\"final error sending batch\", \"status\", status)\n   325→\t\tc.metrics.droppedBytes.WithLabelValues(c.cfg.URL.Host).Add(bufBytes)\n Here's the function:\n\n```go\nfunc (q *QuerierAPI) InstantQueryHandler(ctx context.Context, req *queryrange.LokiInstantRequest) (logqlmodel.Result, error) {\n\t// do not allow log selector expression (aka log query) as instant query\n\tif _, ok := req.Plan.AST.(syntax.SampleExpr); !ok {\n\t\treturn logqlmodel.Result{}, logqlmodel.ErrUnsupportedSyntaxForInstantQuery\n\t}\n\n\tif err := q.validateMaxEntriesLimits(ctx, req.Plan.AST, req.Limit); err != nil {\n\t\treturn logqlmodel.Result{}, err\n\t}\n\n\tparams, err := queryrange.ParamsFromRequest(req)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn logqlmodel.Result{}, err\n\t}\n\n\tif q.cfgV2.Enable && hasDataObjectsAvailable(q.cfgV2, params.Start(), params.End()) {\n\t\tquery := q.engineV2.Query(params)\n\t\tresult, err := query.Exec(ctx)\n\t\tif err == nil {\n\t\t\treturn result, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tlogger := utillog.WithContext(ctx, q.logger)\n\t\tif !errors.Is(err, engine.ErrNotSupported) {\n\t\t\tlevel.Error(logger).Log(\"msg\", \"query execution failed with new query engine\", \"err\", err)\n\t\t\treturn result, errors.Wrap(err, \"failed with new execution engine\")\n\t\t}\n\t\tlevel.Warn(logger).Log(\"msg\", \"falling back to legacy query engine\", \"err\", err)\n\t}\n\n\tquery := q.engineV1.Query(params)\n\treturn query.Exec(ctx)\n}\n```\n\n## Key Characteristics\n\nThe handler validates that queries use `syntax.SampleExpr` (metric expressions only), rejects log selector expressions, enforces entry limits, and attempts execution via the v2 engine with fallback to the v1 legacy engine if unsupported."}]},"parent_tool_use_id":"toolu_01FcF6WXLMDXT2dDkDHLheRD","session_id":"d91fb030-74c9-4bc0-8b8f-b4fe27d8e889","uuid":"a740559d-d4b0-47eb-837a-d20225f9a482"}
